Motivation and Context
This PR is related to and closes this issue.
Description
This PR implements a feature that adds an autocomplete function for the group names. With that, admins can easily add the respective group names to the users preventing non-existent groups from being added.
Steps for Testing
Prerequisites:

1 admin user
1 existing non-admin user


Log in to Artemis as admin
Navigate to Server Administration
Choose User Management
Select a user and try to add the user to a group
Observe adding existing/non-existing groups to the user
Save and make sure that the group is added to the user

                                                                            <h3 dir="auto">Motivation and Context</h3>
                                                                            <p dir="auto">This PR is related to and closes this <a href="https://github.com/ls1intum/Artemis/issues/6587" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/ls1intum/Artemis/issues/6587/hovercard">issue</a>.</p>
                                                                            <h3 dir="auto">Description</h3>
                                                                            <p dir="auto">This PR implements a feature that adds an autocomplete function for the group names. With that, admins can easily add the respective group names to the users preventing non-existent groups from being added.</p>
                                                                            <h3 dir="auto">Steps for Testing</h3>
                                                                            <p dir="auto">Prerequisites:</p>
                                                                            <ul dir="auto">
                                                                                <li>1 admin user</li>
                                                                                <li>1 existing non-admin user</li>
                                                                            </ul>
                                                                            <ol dir="auto">
                                                                                <li>Log in to Artemis as admin</li>
                                                                                <li>Navigate to Server Administration</li>
                                                                                <li>Choose User Management</li>
                                                                                <li>Select a user and try to add the user to a group</li>
                                                                                <li>Observe adding existing/non-existing groups to the user</li>
                                                                                <li>Save and make sure that the group is added to the user</li>
                                                                            </ol>
                                                                            <h3 dir="auto">Review Progress</h3>
                                                                            <h4 dir="auto">Performance Review</h4>
